      /* quick sort */
      2
      

      3
      /* quick sort is now done over lists with tail pointer
      

      4
         so that append can be done in constant time */
      

      5
      

      6
      data node {
      

      7
      	int val; 
      

      8
      	node next; 
      

      9
      }
      

      10
      

      11
      // sorted lseg
      

      12
      lseg == self=p & n=0 & sm<=lg
      

      13
      		or self::node * r::lseg & sm<=sm1<=lg
      

      14
      	inv n >= 0 & sm<=lg;
      

      15
      

      16
      // sorted list with tail
      

      17
      ll_tail == self::node & t=self & n=1 & sm=lg
      

      18
      		or self::node * r::ll_tail & r!=null & sm<=sm1
      

      19
      	inv n>=0 & self!=null;
      

      20
      

      21
      // bounded list with tail
      

      22
      bnd_tail == self = null & n = 0 & t=null & sm <= lg
      

      23
      	or self::node & t = self & n = 1 & sm <= v <= lg
      

      24
      	or self::node * p::bnd_tail & sm <= d <= lg & p!=null
      

      25
      inv n >= 0;
      

      26
      

      27
      

      28
      coercion "ll_tail2lseg" self::ll_tail <-> self::lseg * t::node & lg1<=lg;
      

      29
      

      30
      /*
      

      31
      coercion "lsegmb" self::lseg <-> self::lseg * q::lseg & n=n1+n2 & lg1<=sm2; 
      

      32
      */
      

      33
      

      34
      coercion "lsegmb" self::lseg & n = n1+n2 & n1,n2 >=0  <-> self::lseg * q::lseg & lg1<=sm2;
      

      35
      

      36
      

      37
      void qsort(ref node x, ref node tx)
      

      38
      	requires x::bnd_tail & n>0
      

      39
      	ensures x'::ll_tail & sm <= sm1 & lg1 <= lg & m = n ;
      

      40
      {
      

      41
      	if (x == null) return; // not needed
      

      42
      	else if (x.next == null) {
      

      43
            //assume false;
      

      44
      		return;
      

      45
      	}
      

      46
      	else {
      

      47
      		node y, ty, tmp1;
      

      48
      		int temp = x.val;
      

      49
      

      50
      		assert x'::bnd_tail & sm <= temp' <= lg;
      

      51
      		assert x'::bnd_tail<_, tx', sm, lg> & sm <= temp' <= lg;
      

      52
                      dprint;
      

      53
      		partition1(x, tx, y, ty, x.val);
      

      54
      

      55
      		// recursive sorting
      

      56
      

      57
      		if (x != null)
      

      58
      			qsort(x, tx);
      

      59
      

      60
      		if (y != null)
      

      61
      			qsort(y, ty);
      

      62
      

      63
      		if (x == null) {
      

      64
                //assume false;
      

      65
      			x = y;
      

      66
      			tx = ty;
      

      67
                  assert x'::ll_tail;
      

      68
      			return;
      

      69
      		}
      

      70
      		else if (y != null) {
      

      71
      			tx.next = y;
      

      72
      			tx = ty;
      

      73
                  //dprint;
      

      74
                  assert x'::ll_tail<_, _, _, _>; //'
      

      75
                    //assume false;
      

      76
      			return;
      

      77
      		}
      

      78
      	}
      

      79
      }
      

      80
      

      81
      /*
      

      82
      	partitions a list pointed to by x to 
      

      83
      	two lists. The new x list contains the smaller elements, the y list
      

      84
      	contains the bigger ones.
      

      85
      */	
      

      86
      void partition1(ref node x, ref node tx, ref node y, ref node ty, int c)
      

      87
      	requires x::bnd_tail & sm <= c <= lg 
      

      88
      	ensures x'::bnd_tail * y'::bnd_tail & n=n1+n2;
      

      89
      {
      

      90
      	if (x == null) {
      

      91
      		tx = null;
      

      92
      		ty = null;
      

      93
      		y = null;
      

      94
      		return; //FIXIT: accept return null
      

      95
      	}
      

      96
      	else {
      

      97
      		int v; 
      

      98
      

      99
      		if (x.val < c) {
      

      100
      			// x belongs to the first partition (the smaller one)
      

      101
      			if (x.next == null) {
      

      102
      				tx = x; // shoudlnt' be needed
      

      103
      				ty = null;
      

      104
      				y = null;
      

      105
      				return;
      

      106
      			}
      

      107
      			else {
      

      108
      				bind x to (xval, xnext) in {
      

      109
      					partition1(xnext, tx, y, ty, c);
      

      110
      				}
      

      111
      

      112
      				if (x.next == null) {
      

      113
      					// If all the rest goes to the second list, 
      

      114
      					// the first list contains only one element.
      

      115
      					// After the recursive partition call, tx is null,
      

      116
      					// hence need to set it to point to x
      

      117
      					tx = x;
      

      118
      				}
      

      119
      

      120
      				return;
      

      121
      			}
      

      122
      		}
      

      123
      		else {
      

      124
      			if (x.next == null) {
      

      125
      				y = x;
      

      126
      				ty = x;
      

      127
      				x = null;
      

      128
      				tx = null;
      

      129
      				return;
      

      130
      			}
      

      131
      			else {
      

      132
      				bind x to (xval, xnext) in {
      

      133
      					partition1(xnext, tx, y, ty, c);
      

      134
      				}
      

      135
      

      136
      				// xs  belongs to the "greater than" partition, which is pointed
      

      137
      				// to by y.
      

      138
      				// xs must be updated to point to the "greater than" partition.
      

      139
      

      140
      				if (y == null) ty = x;
      

      141
      	
      

      142
      				node tmp1 = x;
      

      143
      				x = x.next;
      

      144
      

      145
      				tmp1.next = y;
      

      146
      				y = tmp1;
      

      147
      

      148
      

      149
      				return;
      

      150
      			}
      

      151
      		}
      

      152
      	}
      

      153
      }
